|cffff8000育母蜘蛛|r |cffb8860bVX模式需要在她产卵的时候不破坏任何卵.
|cffff8000Broodmother|r |cffb8860bcan be killed with VX mode if you won't kill any of the eggs she spawns.
|cffff8000纳瑞斯|r |cffb8860bVX模式需要在不破坏任何元素容器的情况下将纳瑞斯打至75%生命值以下.
|cffff8000Narith|r |cffb8860bcan be killed with VX mode if you focus Narith and you won't kill any of the containers.
|cffff8000沙魔像|r |cffb8860bVX模式需要在不杀死任何迷你岩石傀儡的情况下击杀沙魔像.
|cffff8000Sand Golem|r |cffb8860bcan be killed with VX mode if you kill him without killing any of the shardlings.
|cffff8000克里克斯|r |cffb8860bVX模式需要先杀死5只小蝎子, 在克里克斯的生命值95%以上. 如果克里克斯被攻击至95%生命以下, 小蝎子就会消失. 一定时间内没有杀光5只小蝎子, 小蝎子也会消失, 不进入VX模式.
|cffff8000Karrix|r |cffb8860bcan be killed with VX mode if you kill 5 baby scorpions just right after you enter the room. I advise you to ignore Karrix before you kill them all. Else they will disappear.
|cffff8000阿诺斯|r |cffb8860bVX模式需要在4个角落召唤出小火人, 杀死全部4个小火人后进入VX模式.
|cffff8000Avnos|r |cffb8860bcan be killed with VX mode if you spawn the Fire Orb and kill Avnos after it. To spawn the Fire Orb, you need to kill 4 minions. To summon a minion, come close to the firey corner.
|cffff8000卡诺思|r |cffb8860bVX模式需要需要让卡诺思被暴风雪淋50次产生冰霜效果. 效果不会持续太久, 你需要迅速杀死卡诺思或者让其再淋一次暴风雪来重置冰霜效果时间.
|cffff8000Karnos|r |cffb8860bcan be killed with VX mode if you make him stack Frostbite 50 times. Stacks will reset if Karnos won't get them for long, so take this into consideration.
|cffff8000卡拉诺斯|r |cffb8860bVX模式需要所有的人在P1叠加35层BUFF, 可以是冰,火或者双重. 记住, 所有人都要叠BUFF.

帮助: 命令
Help: Commands
可使用指令:
Chat commands:
-rewards|r 查看你完成但是还没有领取奖励的任务.会在小地图标记NPC的位置.
-rewards|r displays every quest you have completed, but have not claimed your reward. Also pings the NPC on the minimap that gives the reward.
-qitems|r 查看哪个玩家持有任务物品.
-qitems|r displays what player carries what quest items.
-fog|r 开关雾效果.
-fog|r turns off/on the fog system.
-music|r 开关音乐.
-music|r turns off/on the music system.
-roll|r 获得一个1-100间的随机数.
-roll|r rolls a random 1-100 for fair loot splitting.
-rm|r 重置对你的 DPS/HPS 统计.
-rm|r resets the damage/healing meters for your hero.
-goodbye|r 当出现(NULL)对话错误时,强制中止对话.
-goodbye|r emergancy exit of chat when a (NULL) error occurs.
-cview|r 切换视角锁定.
-cview|r cycle through game camera options.
-cdist|r 改变视角距离.
-cdist|r cycle through camera distance options.
-hicons|r 开关左侧的英雄头像.
-hicons|r turn on the left side hero portraits.
帮助: 操作菜单
Help: Action Menu
动作菜单:
Actions Menu:
按下N或者点击动作菜单按钮(红十字)将会在你的物品栏里打开动作菜单. 你可以做以下操作:
Pushing N or clicking the Actions spell will open a menu in your hero's inventory. From here several things are possible:
交谈:|r 和NPC自由交谈, 获得线索, 故事, 或者任务.
Talk:|r talks to NPC's for random chat, possible hints, story, or to get quests.
互动:|r 打开一个显示你可进行的互动操作的子菜单.
Interact:|r Opens a sub-menu with different possible interactions you can perform.
角色管理:|r 查看天赋树或者装备栏.
Character Management:|r Opens a sub-menu for managing your characters talent trees or equipment.
查看属性:|r 打开属性界面分配你的属性点.
View Sub-Stats:|r Opens a sub-menu for managing your characters stat points.
游戏选项:|r 调整游戏选项.
Game Options:|r Opens a sub-menu for changing game options.
关闭动作菜单:|r 关闭动作菜单,返回通常的物品栏.
Close Actions:|r exits the actions menu and returns to your heroes normal inventory.
帮助: 装备
Help: Equipment
如何装备物品:
How to equip items:
当你捡起装备时,他会进入你的装备背包,而不是默认的魔兽3的物品栏.
When an item that can be equipped is picked up, it goes into your hero's equipment inventory, not the standard WC3 inventory.
动作菜单 -> 角色管理 -> 装备栏
Actions -> Character Management -> Show Equipment
这样你就能打开装备栏了, 指向一个装备可以查看其属性, 左键单击选中, 随后点击你想装备的位置. 请注意装备需求: 等级, 属性, 类型等等.
Here you will list a list of every equippable item you have picked up as well as what you have on. Hovering over an item will display its properties, left click it to highlight, then left click on the slot you wish to equip it to. Please pay attention to item requirements: Level, stats required, proficiency and so on.
帮助: 天赋树
Help: Talent Tree
如何分配天赋点:
How to spend talent points:
当你开始游戏时, 你没有技能但是有1个天赋点.
When you start the game, you have 0 abilities and 1 talent point.
动作菜单 -> 角色管理 -> 天赋树
Actions -> Character Management -> Show Talent Tree
在这里你可以查看你的天赋树并分配天赋点.左边通常是技能相关天赋.指向天赋来查看效果.
Here you will find your character's talent tree and all the available talents you can eventually learn. The left tree is your ability tree. Hover over a talent to see what it is and its effects.
帮助: 基本知识
Help: Basic Knowledge
基本知识:
Common Knowledge:
-技能不会升级. 你开始的1天赋点可以用来学习技能. 所有的技能都会受到某种属性的影响.
-There are no skill upgrades. You start with 1 talent point which can be used to learn abilities. All of your hero's abilities are determined by your stats directly. Each spell states what effects it.
-每2级会获得1天赋点(2级, 4级, 6级, 8级, 等等)
-You gain 1 talent point every 2 levels (2, 4, 6, 8, etc)
-怪物的生命值,伤害,攻击速度,以及掉落物品都会受到游戏人数和人物职业的影响.
-Monster HP, damage, attack speed, and loot is all effected by how many players there are in the game and what type of classes the players are.
-出现记录码时请截图保存来避免错误,或者使用代码记录器.各大城市都有保存英雄的NPC.
-Be sure to screen shot the password to avoid copy errors or use GameCapture (see forum for details). Hero savers are located in every major city.
-当你进入一个新的区域,你也许见不到很多怪物,但是随着时间的流逝,会产生越多怪物.
-When you first enter a zone, you may not see many monsters, but the longer you stay in it, the more will spawn.

盾击
Shield Slam

冲锋
Charge
学习冲锋: 冲向目标对其造成伤害并击退, 伤害所有冲锋路径的敌人
Teaches Charge: Charges the target dealing damage and knocking it back. Also deals damage to all units in the path of the charge
破胆怒吼
Intimidating Bellow
学习破胆怒吼: 伤害一个敌人, 使其移动速度降低15%, 降低目标攻击力12%
Teaches Intimidating Bellow: Cripples an enemy by lowering its movement speed by 15% and its attack damage by 12%
攻击姿态
Aggressive Stance
战士获得攻击姿态. 不能学习防御姿态, 而且不能格挡. 战斗命令效果减少60%. 免伤5%. 提高等级相关的攻强. 
Cannot learn Defensive Stance. Block Chance is fixed at 0%. All damage dealt will be increased. All damage received will be reduced by 5%. Battle Orders effect will be reduced by 60%.
防御姿态
Defensive Stance
战士获得防御姿态. 不能学习攻击姿态. 提高仇恨, 免伤5%.
Cannot learn Aggressive Stance. Dramatically increases aggro generation and reduces all damage taken by 5%.
旋风斩
Whirlslash
学习旋风斩: 对自身周围敌人造成物理伤害
Teaches Whirlslash: Multi target area effect attack that deals physical damage
战斗命令
Battle Orders
学习战斗命令: 使友军获得生命值上限提升的BUFF
Teaches Battle Orders: Increases the HP of all the heroes around when used
英勇怒吼
Heroic Shout
学习英勇怒吼: 对周围敌人获得大量仇恨, 并短暂增加战士伤害减免55%
Teaches Heroic Shout: Grants the warrior 55% damage reduction for the duration and generates threat on all nearby enemies
强化盾击
Improved Shield Slam
短暂击晕敌人. 如果目标不能被击晕, 造成*0/16/32/48*%额外伤害. 第三点: 防御姿态在1.5秒内反射物理伤害. 攻击姿态在1秒内提高自己 物理暴击伤害100%.
Stuns the target for a short duration, or *0/16/32/48*% damage if target can't be stunned.^Third point: Reflects physical damage for 1.5 seconds if in Defensive Stance. Adds attack crit power 100% for 1 second if in Aggressive Stance.
强化冲锋
Improved Charge
防御姿态: 嘲讽目标敌人. 攻击姿态: 等级30级以上, 大幅度提高冲锋伤害.
Defensive Stance: Taunts the enemy.^Aggressive Stance: If hero level is 30 or more, greatly increases Charge damage.
强化破胆怒吼
Improved Intimidating Bellow
降低敌人攻速 20%. 防御姿态: 每次普通攻击降低*0/1/2/3*%攻击速度. 最高10层. 攻击姿态: 持续时间会变成*0/5/8/11*秒, 同时每秒造成*0/10/15/20*%流血伤害.
Lowers the enemy's attack speed by 20%.^Defensive Stance: Each normal attack on affected enemy further reduces *0/1/2/3*% attack speed, stacking up to 10 times.^Aggressive Stance: Causes *0/10/15/20*% bleed damage per second, lasts *0/5/8/11* seconds.
指挥大师
Master Commander
第一点: 战斗命令将提高魔法, 战士每次普攻暴击 回复3点魔法. 第二点: 战士每回复30点魔法, 为周围友军回复30点魔法.
First point: Battle Orders now increases mana and causes the Warrior to regain 3 mana with every critical strike.^Second point: Every time the Warrior regenerates 30 total mana, surrounding friendly units recover 30 mana.
强化旋风斩
Improved Whirlslash
如果目标被盾击击中, 旋风斩造成 *0/85*% 额外伤害. 如果战士拥有进攻姿态, ,敌人被破胆怒吼则提高25%伤害.
Whirlslash now does *0/85*% more damage to targets stunned by Shield Slam. It also adds 25% more damage to target if target is under the effects of Intimidating Bellow and Aggressive Stance is active.
强化英勇怒吼
Improved Heroic Shout
400 半径内的所有友军获得一个40%减伤的 BUFF
All allies within a 400 radius of the warrior get a 40% damage reduction buff
回避
Avoidance
提高闪避率*0/3.75/7.5*%
Increases your dodge chance by *0/3.75/7.5*%
化解
Mitigation
提高格挡率*0/6/12*%
Increases your block chance by *0/6/12*%
狮心
Lionheart
每等级获得 *0/0.075/0.15*% 物理暴击率, *0/0.30/0.60*% 物理暴击伤害.
Increases *0/0.075/0.15*% Attack Crit Chance per hero level, *0/0.30/0.60*% Attack Crit Power per hero level.
自然抵抗
Natural Resistance
提高魔法抗性*0/4/8*%. 防御姿态: 提高等级相关生命回复. 攻击姿态: 获得自然附魔. 提高攻击速度*0/7.5/15*% + 等级的*0/15/30*% .
Increases magic resist by *0/4/8*%.^Defensive Stance: Increases life regeneration.^Aggressive Stance: Increase attack speed by *0/7.5/15*% + *0/15/30*% of hero level.
战斗经验
Battle Veteran
提高力量*0/10/20/30*%的攻击强度. 提高仇恨获取 *0/2/4/6*%.
Increases your attack power by *0/10/20/30*% of your Power. Also increases all threat by *0/2/4/6*%.
盾袭
Shield Spike
提高盾击的伤害*0/15/30*%
Increases damage dealt by Shield Slam by *0/15/30*%
超级冲锋/死亡冲锋
Mega Charge/Devastating Charge
防御姿态: 冲锋後短暂提高战士移动速度100点.^攻击姿态: 充能4秒冲向目标连续造成7次强力攻击.
Defensive Stance: Increases Warrior's move speed by 100 after charging.^Aggressive Stance: Charge will now have 4 second charging time, rushing to the target and striking it 7 times, dealing damage each strike.
指挥艺术
Commanding Presence
提高战斗命令的效果*0/12/24/36*%
Increases the effectiveness of Battle Orders by *0/12/24/36*%
进阶英勇怒吼
Empowered Heroic Shout
增加英勇怒吼的持续时间*0/0.667/1.33/2* 秒
Increases the duration of Heroic Shout by *0/0.667/1.33/2* seconds
顺势斩
Cleave
学习顺势斩: 对目标周围的敌人, 造成普通攻击伤害值70%的物理伤害
Teaches Cleave: Causes autoattacks to deal 70% of their damage in a small AoE around the target. Drains mana with every hit.
重斩
Deep Slice
学习重斩: 单体物理攻击
Teaches Deep Slice: A single target attack that deals physical damage
战嚎
Warcry
学习战嚎: 增加周围友军的攻击力
Teaches Warcry: A shout that increases the autoattack damage of all nearby allied units
战狂之怒
Berserker Rage
使得你的每次普攻伤害都会增加. 8次攻击后积累的能量将被释放造成一次巨大伤害. 同时提升你5%的移动速度
Teaches Berserker Rage: A buff that causes your normal attacks to increase your damage. After 8 attacks the built up charges are unleashed for a powerful damaging strike. You also move 5% faster
战斗饥渴
Battle Lust
学习战斗饥渴: 使得周围友军普通攻击时获取生命值
Teaches Battle Lust: A shout that causes all nearby allied units to gain health whenever they attack
剑刃风暴
Bladestorm
学习剑刃风暴: 降低你的移动速度40%, 不能使用技能, 但是每0.5秒对周围敌人造成致命的伤害
Teaches Bladestorm: A deadly move that reduces your movement speed by 40% and disables your other spells but does powerful damage to all nearby enemies every half second
强化重斩
Improved Deep Slice
重斩造成流血效果, 每秒造成基础伤害14%的持续伤害
Deep Slice now applies a bleed effect to the target for 14% of Deep Slice's base damage per tick

Warcry now inceases the health regeneration of units

将同时提高野蛮人*0/22/44*%的攻击速度
Berserker Rage will incrase your attack speed by *0/22/44*% as well
强化战斗饥渴
Improved Battle Lust
战斗饥渴将提高物理和法术暴击率
Battle Lust now increases your attack and spell critical strike chances
强化剑刃风暴
Improved Bladestorm
剑刃风暴提高 目标受到的任何伤害 *0/5/10*%, 并且使你获得*0/10/20*%的免伤.
Bladestorm now makes hit units take *0/5/10*% more damage from all sources and you take *0/10/20*% less damage while active.

Battle Fury

Increases attack power by *0/10/20/30*% of your Power. Increases Attack Speed by *0/5/10/15*% + *0/10/20/30*% of your hero level.

Increases your attack crit chance by *0/3/6/9*%. Increases Attack Damage by *0/30/60/90*% of your hero level.

Armor Piercing

Increases your attack crit power by *0/10/20/30*% + *0/0.1/0.2/0.3*% per level.

进阶剑刃风暴
Empowered Bladestorm
剑刃风暴的伤害提高 *0/12/24/36*%, 使敌人受到额外伤害加成 *0/3/6/9*%, 移动速度奖励变为 *-40/-20/0/20*%. 提高无人生还 眩晕时间 *0/0.5/1.0/1.5* 秒.
Increases Bladestorm's damage by *0/12/24/36*% and the extra damage enemies take by *0/3/6/9*% and change the move speed bonus to *-40/-20/0/20*%. Increases No One Lives stun time by *0/0.5/1.0/1.5* seconds.
野性
Wild Might
德鲁伊: 月火术 - 单体魔法伤害^熊: 撞槌 - 单体物理伤害^狼: 撕咬 - 单体物理伤害^树人: 回春术 - 持续回复生命
Druid: Moonfire - Single target magic attack^Bear: Maul - Single target physical attack^Wolf: Bite - Single target physical attack^Treant: Rejuvenation - Heal over time
大地之力
Earthen Strength
德鲁伊: - 纠缠根须: 单体定身和伤害^熊: 粉碎 - 范围物理伤害^狼: 怒意狂击 - 前方范围物理伤害^树人: 树肤术 - 增加护甲
Druid: - Earthen Grasp: Single target root attack^Bear: Crush - Physical area attack^Wolf: Fury Swipes - Physical frontal area attack^Treant: Barkskin - Armor buff
月之能量
Power of the Moon
德鲁伊: 星落 - 范围持续魔法伤害^熊: 狂暴 - 增加攻强持续消耗生命值^狼: 嗥叫 - 范围降低敌人命中和移动速度^树人: 愈合之触 - 单体治疗
Druid: Starfall - Magical area damage attack^Bear: Enrage - Increase Power at cost of Life per second^Wolf: Howl - Area debuff that lowers hit chance and movement speed^Treant: Mending Touch - A direct heal
形态转换
Shapeshifting
学习形态转换: 德鲁伊可以在多型态中切换: 熊, 狼, 树人. 每种形态都有不同的技能, 这可以改变德鲁伊的玩法.^德鲁伊和树人基于法强. 狼和熊基于攻强.
Teaching Shapeshifting: The druid learns how to shift into multiple forms: Bear, Wolf, Treant. Each form enables certain key abilities and alters the druid's playstyle.^Druid and Treant forms are SP based.^Wolf and Bear forms are AP based.
自然精通
Natural Mastery
德鲁伊: 水之精华 - 激活后增加目标的法术强度 10%^熊: 冬眠 - 不能使用技能并增加护甲和魔法抗性, 结束后回复生命值和魔法值^狼: 突袭 - 跳跃至单体目标并造成物理伤害^树人: 和平之心 - 一个增益效果, 激活后增加目标的治疗能力
Druid: Essence of Water - Increases target's spell power by 10% while active^Bear: Hibernate - Limits your abilities for a defense boost and restores hp and mana^Wolf: Pounce - Leap to the target and attack, or reduces damage and gives haste to an ally^Treant: Peaceful Mind - Increases all healing done by the target while active
强化野性
Improved Wild Might
德鲁伊: 强化月火术 - 给予目标一个DEBUFF, 下次非DOT魔法伤害提升10%^熊: 强化撞槌 - 给予目标一个DEBUFF, 其受到更多的粉碎伤害. 每20秒可以强制获得仇恨一次^狼: 强化撕咬 - 给予目标一个DEBUFF, 叠加5次后造成4次流血伤害^树人: 强化回春术 - 在持续时间结束后, 会弹射给附近的一个友军
Druid: Improved Moonfire - Adds a debuff so the next magical attack does 10% more damage^Bear: Improved Maul - Adds a debuff to take more damage from Crush and reaggroes the target once in 20s.^Wolf: Improved Bite - Stacking debuff applies bleed on the 5th stack of Bite^Treant: Improved Rejuvenation - On end applies Lesser Rejuvenation to a nearby ally
强化大地之力
Improved Earthen Strength
德鲁伊: 强化纠缠根须 - 可以缠绕目标周围300范围内的敌人^熊: 强化粉碎 - 使敌人获得命中下降的DEBUFF^狼: 强化怒意狂击 - 使目标受到额外的物理伤害^树人: 强化树肤术 - 树肤术还可以减伤
Druid: Improved Earthen Grasp - Nearby enemies in 300 radius are also rooted^Bear: Improved Crush - Also lowers target's hit chance^Wolf: Improved Fury Swipes - Debuffs the target to take 15% more attack damage^Treant: Improved Barkskin - Barkskin now also reduces damage taken
强化月之能量
Improved Power of the Moon
德鲁伊: 强化星落 - 对中月火术的目标伤害增加50%^熊: 强化狂暴 - 激活后增加撞槌和粉碎的伤害20%^狼: 强化嗥叫 - 增加持续时间5秒和15%命中下降的DEBUFF^树人: 强化愈合之触 -对有回春术的目标施放治疗量增加20%
Druid: Improved Starfall - Increases damage by 50% on targets with Moonfire^Bear: Improved Enrage - Increases Maul and Crush damage by 20% while active^Wolf: Improved Howl - Increases duration by 5s and chance to miss by 15%^Treant: Improved Mending Touch - Rejuvination buffs increase healing by 20% each
强化形态转换
Improved Shapeshifting
熊: 增加护甲, 生命和格挡^狼: 增加暴击和30移动速度^树人: 增加魔法回复, 智力和5%魔法抗性
Bear: Grants bonus armor, health, and block^Wolf: Bonus to criticals and 30 move speed^Treant: Bonus mana per second, energy and 5% magical damage reduction
强化自然精通
Improved Natural Mastery
德鲁伊: 强化水之精华 - 可以增加最大魔法值^熊: 强化冬眠 - 施法中获得周围敌人大量仇恨. 技能结束后15秒内增加生命回复, 攻击速度和移动速度^狼: 强化突袭 - 撕咬可以眩晕目标^树精: 强化和平之心 - 增加1点每秒的魔法回复
Druid: Improved Essence of Water - Also increases maximum mana pool^Bear: Improved Hibernate - On cast, aggroes all enemies in large AoE. On end, 15s Rested buff gives Power, Attack Speed and Move Speed^Wolf: Improved Pounce - Now stuns the target and applies bite buff^Treant: Improved Peaceful Mind - Now also adds 1 mana per second regen
活力
Vigor
提高力量和敏捷的*0/4/8/12*%的攻强, 提高智力*0/8/16/24*%的法强. 任何二级光环每秒都有*1/2/3*% 概率解除范围内队友异常状态.
Increases Attack Power by *0/4/8/12*% of your Power and Agility and increases Spell Power by *0/8/16/24*% of your Energy.^Any aura has a *0/1/2/3*% chance per second to cancel negative effect of allies in range.
自然缤纷
Nature's Diversity
第一点: 所有形态都用攻强/法强的77%/68%相加来计算混合强度, 而不是100%/0%.^第二点: 所有形态都用物理/法术暴击率和暴击伤害的60%/60%相加来计算混合暴击率和暴击伤害, 而不是100%/0%.^熊狼以攻强为主, 人树以法强为主
First point: Use a hybrid mix of 77%/68% AP and SP in each form, instead of 100%/0%.^Second point: Your critical chance and power for abilities is a hybrid mix of 60%/60% of attack and spell, instead of 100%/0%.
进阶野性
Empowered Wild Might
德鲁伊: 月火术增加*0/6/12/18*%的伤害和*0/15/30/45*%的溅射伤害.^熊: 撞槌增加伤害 *0/14/28/42*%.^狼: 撕咬增加*0/10/20/30*%的伤害和流血伤害.^树人: 回春术持续时间增加*0/1/2/3*秒.
Druid: Moonfire deals *0/6/12/18*% more damage and *0/15/30/45*% splash damage.^Bear: Maul deals *0/14/28/42*% more damage.^Wolf: Bite deals *0/10/20/30*% more damage and bleed.^Treant: *0/1/2/3* sec longer Rejuv.

Druid: Earthen Grasp deals *0/16/32/48*% more damage.^Bear: Crush deals *0/11/22/33*% more damage.^Wolf: Fury Swipes deals *0/13/26/39*% more damage.^Treant: Barkskin lasts *0/5/10/15*s longer whenever the target receives a treant spell; cap of 5 extension per cast.

形态精通
Form Mastery
第一点: 取消变身虚弱及变身冷却时间^第二点: 变身后可以获得月之祝福, 在5秒内提高攻击强度, 法术强度, 闪避5%^第三点: 变身后立刻回复30点魔法值
First point: Removes Weakening and resetting cooldown of Shapeshift.^Second point: After shapeshifting, grants a buff that increases AP, SP, and Dodge by 5% for 5 seconds^Third point: Shapeshifting regenerates 30 mana.

平静
Serenity
学习平静: 一个范围*0/600/800/1000*的光环, 提高友军魔法抗性*0/8/12/16*%. 提高自身魔法抗性*0/12/16/20*%, 每级光环提高更多攻击和法术强度. 第三点: 获得10秒一次的自动月火术^多个光环不能叠加.
Teaches Serenity: A *0/600/800/1000* AOE party aura that increases magic resist by *0/8/12/16*%. Druid himself gets *0/12/16/20*% extra magic resist and bonus SP and AP.^Third point: Autocast Moonfire once every 10 seconds^Multiple auras do not stack.
狂热
Frenzy
学习狂热: 被动状态, 当熊形态生命值低于60%时激活.^提高等级x*0/1.2/1.6/2.0*生命回复, 提高等级x*0/0.3/0.4/0.5*%魔法抗性. 提高等级x*0/1.2/1.6/2.0*%的攻击速度 提高*0/15/25/35*移动速度, 提高*0/5/8/11*%格挡. 第二点: 获得600范围光环. 提高友军力量. 第三点: 光环同时提高友军生命回复.^多个光环不能叠加.
Teaches Bear Frenzy: A self buff passive that is activated whenever the Bear has 60% or less health.^Increases hp regen by level x *0/1.2/1.6/2.0*, magic resist by *0/0.3/0.4/0.5*% per level, attack speed by *0/1.2/1.6/2.0*% per level, *0/15/25/35* movespeed, *0/5/8/11*% block.^Second point: Emits 600 AoE aura that adds power.^Third point: Aura also adds life regen.^Multiple auras do not stack.
狼王
Pack Leader
学习狼王: 一个范围*0/600/800/1000*的光环, 提高等级x*0/0.8/1.2/1.6*攻击强度. 提高等级x*0/0.4/0.7/1.0*的敏捷. 狼获得20%额外加成. 第二点: 光环附加移动速度. 第三点: 狼有30%概率刷新怒意狂击.^多个光环不能叠加.
Teaches Pack Leader: A *0/600/800/1000* AOE party aura that adds *0/0.8/1.2/1.6* AP per hero level, AGI by *0/0.4/0.7/1.0* per level. The wolf gets 1.2x effect from this aura.^Second point: Adds movespeed as well.^Third point: Wolf has a 30% chance to ignore Fury Swipes cooldown.^Multiple auras do not stack.
宁静
Tranquility
学习树人光环: 一个范围1200的的光环, 每*0/8/6/4*秒治疗所有友军. 治疗量随光环等级提升而略微降低. 第三点: 光环回复友军魔法值.^多个树光环可以叠加.
Teaches Treant Aura: A 1200 AOE party aura that heals all party members every *0/8/6/4* seconds. Aura heal is slightly lowered as this talent is increased.^Third point: Also restores some mana.^Multiple Tranquility auras can stack.

Teaches Remorseless Strike: A single target attack that deals physical damage. Performs bonus effects and restores mana based on which debuffs the Phantom Stalker has on the target^Damage for Gash, damage and stun for Puncture, and spreads the poison to nearby enemies for Shuriken.

强化混沌诅咒
Improved Chaotic Curse
有*0/22/28/34*%概率 击晕攻击者1秒. 如果目标不能被眩晕 将会受到混沌骑士的额外反击. 每2秒最多反击一次.
Upon dealing magic damage, there is now a *0/22/28/34*% to stun the attacker for 1.5s. If target cannot be stunned, counterattack triggers. Counterattack only occurs at most once every 2 seconds and its damage improves with the talent level.
强化混沌摄取 / 混沌法球
Improved Chaotic Grasp / Chaotic Orb
混沌摄取将造成伤害.伤害会在目标仇恨改变后产生.^学习奥术大师后, 混沌法球会造成一次350范围伤害.
Chaotic Grasp now deals damage. This damage is applied after the threat is altered.^If Arcane Mastery is talented, Chaotic Orb will now release smaller bolts to hit and damage targets in 350 AoE.
混沌力量
Power of the Chaotic
提升力量*0/5/10/15*%的攻击强度和智力*0/11/22/33*%的法术强度
Increases Attack Power by *0/5/10/15*% of your Power and Spell Power by *0/11/22/33*% of your Energy
混合理论
Hybrid Theory
你的法术受到攻强和法强的混合影响, 提升混合的百分比到*55/65/75*%
Your spells use your AP and SP combined, multiplied by a percentage. Increase this percentage to *55/65/75*%
强化盾牌
Shield Training
增加格挡的伤害量*0/6/12*%并且增加格挡率*0/4/8*%
Increases the damage blocked with your shield by *0/6/12*% and increases your chance to block by *0/4/8*%
进阶意念之刃
Empowered Mindblade
提高意念之刃*0/10/20*%的伤害, 且对被破甲的单位造成*0/10/20*%额外伤害
Increases the damage of Mindblade by *0/10/20*% and the bonus damage against targets with Armor Break by *0/10/20*%
混沌攻击
Chaotic Attacks
被意念之刃攻击的敌人 有一定概率被眩晕2秒. 主目标50%概率, 溅射目标20%概率. 如果目标不能被眩晕, 那么他将会受到额外20%的伤害
Targets hit by Mindblade may be stunned for 2s. 50% chance for main target, 20% for AoE targets. If you roll a stun but target cannot be stunned, you get 20% bonus damage instead
破碎护甲
Shattered Armor
提高破甲的效果*0/25/50/75*%
Increases the effectiveness of Armor Break by *0/25/50/75*%

Empowered Hasten / Inspire
提高加速或鼓舞的所有效果20%
Increases the effectiveness of Hasten or Inspire by 20% to all aspects
进阶混沌诅咒
Empowered Chaotic Curse
受到混沌诅咒的敌人, 将会额外受到*0/7/10/13*%伤害, 降低0/5/10/15*%移动速度, 持续4秒.
Chaotic Curse now weakens the attackers causing them to take an additional *0/7/10/13*% damage and reduce *0/5/10/15*% move speed for 4s.
进阶混沌摄取 / 混沌法球
Empowered Chaotic Grasp / Chaotic Orb
提高混沌摄取的伤害*0/250/500*%. 混沌法球提高同样的伤害.
Increases damage from Chaotic Grasp and Chaotic Orb by *0/250/500*%.

Shadow Bind
学习暗影束缚: 诅咒单体目标, 在他每次进行攻击时, 你都可以偷取他的攻击速度. 释放一次黑暗凋零.
Teaches Shadow Bind: Curses the target so that whenever they attack, you drain some of their attack speed. Casts 1 time Dark Blast on the target.
暗影形态
Shadow Form
学习暗影形态: 变身成一个恶魔一段时间, 提高自身攻强和法强.
Teaches Shadow Form: Transforms into a Demon, gaining bonus to Attack Power and Spell Power.
邪恶之触
Unholy Embrace
学习邪恶之触: 诅咒目标, 使目标在诅咒期间内 受到的所有伤害 在结束后将造成 额外百分百的伤害.
Teaches Unholy Embrace: Inclifts a curse on the target that stores all damage dealt to it. When the curse expires, the target takes a percent of all the damage stored.

强化暗影形态
Improved Shadow Form

Shadow Form now bestows its Attack Power and Spell Power bonuses to nearby allies.
强化邪恶之触
Improved Unholy Embrace
邪恶之触诅咒结束后 会治疗目标周围友军, 伤害周围敌军, 平分治疗和伤害.
Unholy Embrace now heals all allies and damage all enemies around the target for a percent of the damage done, split among them.

提高护甲*0/15/30/45*, 并额外提高法术强度*0/3/6/9*%的护甲, 提高闪避*0/4/8/12*%.
Increases your armor by *0/15/30/45* and by *0/3/6/9*% of your spell power. Adds *0/4/8/12*% dodge.
进阶惩戒印记
Empowered M. of R.
提高惩罚印记20%的伤害, 并提高特效触发率 5% + 等级x0.2%
Increases the damage of Mark of Replenishment by 20% and its chances to proc by 5% + 0.2% x hero level.
进阶神圣印记
Empowered M. of S.
取消结束治疗. 前两点分别每秒对范围内友军产生 15%/30%治疗. 第三点恢复结束治疗.
Mark of Sanctuary ticks 1 less time but heals allies in a small AoE for *0/15/30/30*% of healing dealt.^Third point: Restores the 1 lost tick.
进阶圣光术
Empowered Divine Touch
提高圣光术的治疗量和伤害*0/12/24/36*%. 在圣环内治疗量x*0/1.5/2/2.5*.
Increases the healing and damage done by Divine Touch by *0/12/24/36*%. Allies in a holy ring recieve *0/1.5/2/2.5*x healing.
进阶神罚
Empowered Divine Wrath
神罚后在4秒内使普通敌人受到 *0/100/200/300*%额外法术伤害. 对于强力敌人产生法术吸血15%, 持续*0/1/2/3*秒.
Divine Wrath inflicts a debuff that increases damage taken by *0/100/200/300*% only against non-bosses for 4 seconds. Against bosses, instead grants 15% spell lifesteal for *0/1/2/3* seconds.

Increases the damage reduction of Light Infusion by *0/4/8*% and area effect healing by *0/3/6*%

Increases the damage dealt by Divine Light by *0/20/40*% and healing per tick by *0/10/20*% and duration by *0/1/2* seconds.
神圣姿态
Divine Stance
提高圣骑士的仇恨获取. 姿态激活时, 启明之光不能治疗, 但造成2倍伤害. 每次闪避获得额外仇恨.
Increases threat generation. If this talent is learned, Divine Light can no longer heal but its damage is doubled.^Generates threat when dodging attacks.
圣力环绕
Holy Field
启明之光提高移速 *0/25/50/75*. 提高启明之光半径 *0/100/200/300*.^第一点: 圣环会阻止敌人通过.^第二点: 圣光目标脚下产生圣火, 持续快速治疗.^第三点: 圣骑士转化神圣棱镜吸收的伤害为 群体治疗.
Increase Divine Light's AoE by *0/100/200/300*, and allies inside it gain *0/25/50/75* movespeed. First point: Summons a holy ring that repels enemies. Second point: Divine Touch produces holy flame at allies' feet, rapidly healing over time. Third point: Damage received from Holy Prism is converted to healing that is distributed among allies inside Divine Light.
远古护盾
Ancient Shield
学习远古护盾: 对单体友军施加护盾, 减免伤害10% + 0.1%每等级.
Teaches Ancient Shield: Single target allied buff shield that reduces damage taken by 10% + 0.2% x hero level.
温柔治愈
Tender Cure
学习温柔治愈: 治疗单体友军. 如果目标生命值低于 40%, 治疗效果提高 25%.
Teaches Tender Cure: Single target allied spell that heals an ally. If the target has less than 40% of HP remaining, the spell's healing will be increased by 25%.
偿还
Payback
学习偿还: 治疗区域内所有友军.
Teaches Payback: Multi-target area of effect heal which also deals damage in a smaller radius.
同情
Remorse
学习同情: 可开关光环, 持续治疗周围友军并回复魔法, 游医自己会损失魔法.
Teaches Remorse: Toggling aura which increases HP and Mana regeneration of allies near Medicaster. Drains Medicaster's Mana every second.^Heal amount is increased by Mana Prophet multiplier, if any.
自然掠夺
Natural Prey

Teaches Natural Prey: Single target allied buff that gives 20% more aggro generation for selected unit. Increases heals on the target by 10%.
最后机会
Last Chance
学习最后机会: 保护单体有军, 抵抗一次致死伤害.
Teaches Last Chance: Single target allied buff that protects an ally from death once.

混沌洞察
Chaotic Insight
掌握敌人攻击的弱点. 混沌摄取可以 降低敌人攻击造成的伤害 50%. 持续时间与英雄等级相关.
Chaotic Grasp has a chance to reduce enemy attack damage by 50% for a short duration. Duration increases with hero level.
法术折射
Spell Refraction
赎罪为目标添加法术折射盾. 吸收法术伤害, 每次不得超过混强x*0/0.8/1.0/1.2*. 吸收*0/1/2/3*次. BUFF持续10秒. 内置冷却时间20秒.
Cleanse adds a spell reduction shield for 10s.^Reduce next *0/1/2/3* hits of spell damage by *0/0.8/1.0/1.2*x Hybrid Power.^Inner cooldown 20 seconds.
混元体
Mixed Element
混沌姿态: 添加线性伤害吸收50%. 吸收数值不得超过*0/1.3/2.6/3.9*%x最大生命值. 奥术大师: 普通攻击触发混沌法球. 内置冷却时间*0/16/13/10*秒. 第一点: 破甲变为小范围技能. 第二点: 逆转混沌诅咒的负生命回复. 第三点: 混沌骑士格挡的伤害额外提升30%.
Reduce all damage taken by 50%, to a limit of *0/0.013/0.026/0.039* x max Life damage. Arcane Mastery: Autoattack casts Chaotic Orb, inner cooldown *0/16/13/10* sec. First point: Armor Break becomes AoE. Second point: Reverses Chaotic Curse's life drain. Third point: Chaotic Knight takes 30% less damage from blocked attacks.
战斗风暴
Whirlstorm
旋风斩可以让战士每次格挡 *0/60/75/90*%伤害. 提高旋风斩的半径*0/50/100/150*.
Whirlwind sets block damage reduction to *0/60/75/90*% for a short time. Increase Whirlwind radius by *0/50/100/150*.
聆听者
Listener
神秘的声音传达到战士的耳畔. 超级冲锋同时提高自身护甲 等级x*0/1/2/3*. 死亡冲锋斩击造成额外*0/30/60/90*%伤害.
Charge briefly improves armor by level x *0/1/2/3*. Charge deals *0/30/60/90*% more damage if Mega Charge/Devastating Charge is learned.
不动如山 动如雷霆
Indomitable
根据姿态提高或降低仇恨值. 效果随点数增加. 第一点:  超级冲锋粉碎目标装甲5秒. 第二点: 战士连续施展2次盾击才会进入冷却时间. 第三点: 战士的格挡上限提高到80%. 攻击姿态大幅度提高死亡冲锋的伤害.
Increases or decreases threat based on stance. Effect increases with number of points.^First point: Charge reduces enemy armor for 5 sec.^Second point: Shield Slam can be cast twice before entering cooldown.^Third point: Increases max block chance to 80%. If in Aggressive Stance, further improves Charge damage.

夺旗模式
Capture the Flag
进入竞技场, 启动夺旗模式. 夺旗模式具有90%免伤. 每10秒免伤降低1%免伤.  死亡后在场内据点复活. 限时10分钟. 场地中心会出现旗帜. 捡起旗帜并维持. 旗帜在携带英雄死亡后重新回到场地中心, 携带旗帜时间长的队伍获得胜利.
Start the Arena in Capture the Flag mode. All damage will be reduced by 90%. Every 10 seconds a hero isn't in combat drains 1% of their HP. 10 minute limit. The flag will be returned to the center of the field if the carrier dies, and the team with the most captures is victorious.
竞技场不能重复启动
Arena cannot be restarted
杀敌模式
Melee
进入竞技场, 启动杀敌模式. 杀敌模式具有90%免伤. 50%治疗. 每5秒降低1%免伤. 死亡后在场内据点复活. 限时10分钟. 杀敌最多的队伍获得胜利.
Start the Arena in Melee mode. All damage will be reduced by 90%. All healing is reduced by 50%. Every 5 seconds a hero isn't in combat drains 1% of their HP. Heroes can revive after death. 10 minute limit. Defeat the enemy team to be victorious.
竞技模式
Competitive
进入竞技场, 启动竞技模式. 竞技模式下具有初始90%免伤. 治疗量随着时间逐渐减小, 最低10%. 在竞技场效果超过10层后, 生命回复会开始逐层降低, 造成伤害会逐层提高. 最后活下的人所在队伍获得胜利.
Start the Arena in Competitive mode. All damage will be reduced by 90%. Healing will be gradually reduced over time, to a minimum of 10%. If healing is done too often, damage will be taken instead. The last team standing is victorious.

饮血之斧吸取生命值超过自身生命, 转化为护甲. 最大转化英雄等级x*0/2/4/6*点护甲.
Bloody Axe now adds armor when it reaches max effect. Max armor gain is *0/2/4/6* times hero level.
强化灰烬之斧
Improved Ember Strike
灰烬之斧对范围内敌人造成*0/16/32/48*%伤害. 吸引额外仇恨, 与点数相关.
Ember Strike deals *0/16/32/48*% of its damage in an AoE around the target and generates additional threat.^Threat generation increases with talent points spent.
血性狂暴
Blood Rage
提高生命值*0/1/2/3*%的攻击强度.
Increase Attack Power by *0/1/2/3*% of max life.
沸腾之血
Boiling Blood
提高攻击强度*0/15/30/45*%的生命值.
Increases max life by *0/15/30/45*% of Attack Power.
铁血护壁
Iron Blood
副手斧头: 提高英雄等级x*0/0.75/1.5/2.25*护甲. 副手雕像: 提高*0/5/10/15*%格挡.
Adds bonus stats based on the currently equipped offhand.^Dual Axe: Adds hero level x *0/0.75/1.5/2.25* armor.^Idol: Adds *0/5/10/15*% block.
进阶痛击
Empowered Heavystrike
提高痛击伤害*0/20/40/60*%.
Increase Heavystrike damage by *0/20/40/60*%.
炽燃战魂
Burning Spirit
死亡时对周围敌人造成3秒眩晕效果. 目标不能被眩晕则减速100%.
Upon death, nearby enemies are stunned for 3 seconds. Enemies that can't be stunned are slowed by 100%.
进阶裂地
Empowered Fissure
提高沟壑宽度*0/50/100/150*. 裂地消失的时候造成*0/25/50/75*%伤害.
Increases Fissure's width by *0/50/100/150*. When Fissure expires, *0/25/50/75*% of its original damage will be dealt in a small AoE.
法相重生
Rebirth Cycle
重生图腾庇护*0/1/2/3*个友军. 友军死后在图腾处复活, 分别计算冷却时间300秒.
Rebirth Totem affects up to *0/1/2/3* allies. Each ally will have their own separate inner cooldown of 300 seconds.
嗜血狂袭
Blood Strike
图腾重击使队友也获得攻击. 获得*0/20/40/60*%攻击. 第三点使这次攻击吸血.
Nearby allies also receive *0/20/40/60*% of Totem Strike's bonus damage.^Third point: This bonus damage triggers lifesteal.
淘汰之刃
Culling Blade
灰烬之斧斩杀生命值低于*0/10/20/30*%的单位. 造成*0/16/32/48*%的额外伤害. 产生巨大主目标仇恨.
Ember Strike deals *0/16/32/48*% extra damage to enemies below *0/10/20/30*% health. When this effect triggers, additional threat is generated.
法相天地
Roar of the Land
霸体效果. 格挡恢复生命值*0/12/24/36*%x格挡值. 第一点: 普通攻击眩晕对人. 不能眩晕则产生额外仇恨值. 第二点: 友军触碰沟壑获得大地力量, 提高伤害. 第三点: 格挡时提高自身魔抗12%. 持续2秒. 提高队友魔抗: 持续1秒.
When an attack is blocked, heal for *0/12/24/36*% of Block Chance. First point: Normal attack has a small chance to stun target. Generates extra threat on targets that can't be stunned. Second point: Allies in Fissure gain a short damage buff. Third point: Blocking an attack increases magic resist in an AoE by 12% for 2 sec (1 sec for allies).
学习不稳定魔药: 提高一个友军的生命回复. 或对单体敌人造成魔法伤害
Teaches Unstable Potion: Increases the life regeneration of a single ally or deals magic damage to a single enemy
学习治疗波: 发射一道治疗波治疗4个友军, 治疗量逐渐减少
Teaches Healing Chain: Launches a wave of healing energy that bounces, healing up to 4 allies.^Healing is reduced with each bounce.
学习治疗图腾: 创造一个治疗图腾, 每0.5秒治疗周围友军
Teaches Healing Totem: Creates a ward that heals all nearby allies every 0.5 seconds
先祖护佑图腾
Ancestral Blessing Totem
学习先祖护佑图腾: 创造一个先祖庇佑图腾, 提高周围友军最大生命值
Teaches Ancestral Blessing Totem: Summons a totem that improves nearby allies' maximum Life
学习暗影图腾: 创造一个暗影图腾, 高速攻击敌人, 造成魔法伤害
Teaches Shadow Totem: Summons a totem that attacks nearby enemies rapidly, dealing magic damage
学习大地之盾图腾: 创造一个大地之盾图腾, 吸收周围友军受到的伤害
Teaches Earthen Totem: Creates a totem that absorbs damage taken from nearby allies
对友军使用施加BUFF, *0/7/14*%闪避普通攻击. 对敌人使用增加其受到的物理伤害*0/5/10*%.
When used on allies, grants *0/7/14*% dodge. When used on enemies, increases physical damage taken by *0/5/10*%.
第一点: 提高治疗波弹射范围150. 第二点: 治疗波弹射治疗量不会衰减
First point: Increases Healing Chain's AoE by 150.^Second point: Healing Chain will not get weaker each bounce.
治疗图腾同时回复魔法值.
Healing Totem also restores some mana.
暗影武器
Shadow Weapon
普通攻击附带魔法伤害. 减速敌人*0/10/15/20*%. 有*0/10/15/20*%概率击晕敌人. 对不能击晕的单位造成10%额外伤害.
Autoattacks deal additional magic damage and slow enemies by *0/10/15/20*% for a short time, and also have a *0/10/15/20*% chance to stun. Enemies that cannot be stunned take 10% more damage.
嗜血术
Bloodthirst
先祖庇佑图腾对友军施加嗜血术. 提高攻击速度50%, 移动速度75. 内置冷却时间80秒. 持续10秒.
Ancestral Blessing Totem grants Bloodlust on nearby allies, increasing attack speed by 50% and move speed by 75 for 10 seconds.^Inner cooldown 80 seconds.
提高先祖庇佑图腾的范围*0/100/200/300*. 生命上限效果提高*0/10/20/30*%. 提高目标受到的治疗效果*0/5/10/15*%.
Increase Ancestral Blessing Totem's AoE by *0/100/200/300*. Improve max life increase by *0/10/20/30*%. Improve healing received by *0/5/10/15*%.
暗影图腾每攻击15次, 产生一个新的暗影图腾. 最多产生*0/1/2*个.
Shadow Totem creates a new Shadow Totem every 15th attack. This effect can trigger up to *0/1/2* times.^Shadow Totems created by this effect deal 40% of the original's damage.
图腾魔咒
Curse Totem
暗影图腾对攻击目标施加魔咒. 有*0/3/6/9*%使目标攻击无法造成伤害, 持续1秒. 无法施加魔咒则造成*0/10/15/20*额外伤害.
Shadow Totem imposes a debuff on the target that causes it to deal 0 damage on attack at a *0/3/6/9*% rate for 1 second. Enemies immune to this effect instead take *0/10/15/20*% more damage.
提高大地之盾图腾的承受能力*0/20/40*%.
Increase Earthen Totem's durability by *0/20/40*%.
先祖祝福
Blessing of the Ancestors
提高力量+智力*0/5/10/15*%的法术强度.
Increases your Spell Power by *0/5/10/15*% of your Power and Energy.

Shadow Magic

Shadow Veil

Increases Spell Critical Chance by *0/0.075/0.15*% per hero level and Spell Critical Power by *0/0.3/0.6*% per hero level.

Increase Unstable Potion's duration by *0/0.5/1.0/1.5* seconds.

When Earthen Totem is destroyed, nearby enemies suffer a debuff that deals spell damage over time.^Second point: Slows all hit enemies for 5 seconds.
神降术
Descent of the Ancestors
每次施法都会提高法术强度. 可叠加. 最大层数*0/0.1/0.2/0.3*英雄等级. 持续5秒. 第一点: 嗜血术降低内置冷却时间. 第二点: 治疗波传递魔药治疗. 第三点: 暗影萨满受到法术伤害 死亡后可以滞留7秒. 内置冷却时间300秒.
Each spell cast improves Spell Power for *0/3/4/5* sec. This effect stacks up to *0/0.1/0.2/0.3* x level times. First point: When Bloodthirst activates, all inner cooldowns are reduced. Second point: Healing Chain transfers Unstable Potion healing. Third point: Allows hero to survive past death by magic damage for 7 sec, inner cooldown 300 sec

As primitive as the Gnolls are, they still have a command structure. Their current leader goes by the name Razzick. We were inside the cave trying to find the reason for the mutated beasts when we were just overrun by spiders and scorpions. It was horrible, several of my colleagues didn't make it out alive.

你为啥不在洞穴里干掉一些生物呢,这样也许我们能继续我们的调查.
Why don't you head into those caves and thin out the numbers a bit so our teams can actually get some work done, and maybe find the cause of this problem.

In my past travels to Tol'Calm's Cave, I have collected and studied the eggs of the spiders and scorpions, but with the recent mutations, nobody wants to go into that cave, let alone bring me back some of the mutated eggs.
如果你能带给我一些变异卵,也许我能有些新发现来找到事件的起源!
If you can bring me some of the mutated eggs, I can study them and compare my new findings with my old, and maybe figure out some of this mystery!
我和幸存者在洞里的时候,我看到一块具有放射性的晶体,我猜那就是生物变异的原因.
While inside the cave with the surveyors, I discovered a patch of crystals that appeared to have some radioactive properties, I wonder if this is what caused the mutations.
我希望我能在有更多的时间和能力研究那些晶体,然而前提是我能保住命.因此最好的办法是毁掉那晶体.这样也许能中止生物的变异.
I wish I had more time, or the ability to study those crystals without my life being in danger. The best course of action is to just destroy and dispose of that crystal patch. Doing so may bring an end to these mutations.

Gnolls, spiders, and scorpions are actually the least of our worries. Now that you have proven yourself to us, we can entrust you with a bigger task. We can kept this pretty well under wraps for now, but the situation is growing out of hand. Travel down to the garden cloister and see what aid you can lend down there. They will explain the rest to you.
我现在很忙.我得操心我们的战争,有太多需要我谋划的打算的了.如果有问题的话去问牧师们.
I'm a very busy man right now. I am the mastermind for our war efforts, I have lots to plan and strategize for. See one of the priests if you have any questions.
邪恶和危险已经蔓延到大陆的远方.在扎哈拉荒地西边有着兽人们的城市格伦勒,这几周他们一直在被猛烈的沙尘暴袭击.我确定半人马与此事有关.去找塔尔卡门城墙前的骑士达文询问相关情况.我会告诉守卫让你通过的.
This evil and danger stretches far beyond our land. In the Jaharra Barrens to the west lies the orc city of Grom'Gol which has been under attack by a violent sandstorm for several weeks now. I'm sure the centaur have something to do with this. See Knight Davion in the front of the Tol'Calm Wall, he has been assigned to dealing with this matter. I will send word for the guards to let you through the gate.
欢迎来到 沃姆 花园…或者是曾经的花园....
Welcome to the Vormur Gardens... or what's left of them....
死去的灵魂从墓地里复苏了.花园正被邪恶所充斥.我们现在还能挡住他们,但是我们同时还要对付豺狼人.如果你想帮我们,杀掉一些灵魂.
The spirits of our deceased have risen from their graves. The gardens are overrun with evil. We are able to hold them off for now, but our forces are spread thin between the gnolls and now this. If you want to help us, kill off as many of these spirits as you can.
欢迎来到活生生的地狱.凶暴的豺狼人在一边,妖魔鬼怪则在另一边.我们需要任何可能的帮助.
Welcome to my living hell. Fierce Gnolls on one side, angry spirits, ghosts, and zombies on the other. We could use all the extra help we can get right now.
我们不确定其起因或者怎么停下它, 但是我知道有什么强大的玩意需要在它更强大前被阻止.穿过花园和墓穴,你会找到4个拥有特殊力量的僵尸,杀死他们.带上补给品,你会需要的.
We are unsure what caused this or how to stop it, but I do know that there are a few powerful beings that have risen that need to be stopped before they get stronger. Throughout the gardens and catacombs, you will find a few zombies with imbued powers. Seek out and slay them all, there should be 4 of them. Take supplies with you, you will need them.
墓穴里还有一个图书馆,储存着大量历史和知识典籍.我害怕它们大部分都完蛋了...
The catacombs contains a pretty vast library containing much of our history and knowledge. I'm afraid most of it has been lost with this on going battle...
扫除邪恶时优先考虑保护那些典籍.当你在墓地时,尽量收集珍贵的书籍带回来给我.
Preserving our history and knowledge is just as high of a priority as removing this evil. While are you in the catacombs, retrieve as many books as you can and return them to me.
对于这为啥发生我们还知之甚少,但是我们知道其后果.在我们最终解决这神秘事件之前,我们必须清除墓穴里的邪恶生物们.
Not much is known as to why this happened, we just know the aftermath of it. Before we can even begin to solve this mystery, we must remove the evil inside the catacombs.
我已经看过很多被暗影中所滋生的邪恶打败的人了,但是我们不能放弃,我们必须扫清这里的邪恶把这里恢复到原样.前进杀掉那些....东西...有多少杀多少!
I have watched many fall to the evil that lurks within those dark walls, but we cannot give up, we must cleanse that place and remove the evil from it so we can restore it to what it once was. Go forth and kill as many of those.... things... as you can!
沃姆的高级牧师艾瑞森有几个学徒.他们在墓穴深处用魔法努力了很长时间,然而咒语突然出错了,一个学徒的灵魂受了重伤...
Arithan, the High Priest of Vormur, had a few apprentices that he was training. They worked long hours in the depths of the catacombs working on their magic skills and powers. There was an incident with a conjuring spell and one of the apprentice's soul was badly injured. I fear he may be behind this...
事故发生后他再也不一样了,他慢慢滑入了黑暗的深渊.他变得黑暗冷酷并开始学习黑暗魔法.大约一年前,他消失了,现在这些看来就是他干的好事.我们必须解决这个问题.搜寻墓穴看看这是否就是真相.
He was never the same after that accident, he began to slip from reality and the light into the darkness of the abyss. He became a cold and dark person obsessed with the dark arts. He vanished from the temple about a year ago, but what we are seeing here now... looks like his dirty work. We must put an end to this. Search the catacombs and see if this is true.
我听说过很多关于海里的娜迦族的故事,但是我出来没见过.他们一般出现在卡利隆西海岸.
I have heard stories of the sea beasts called Naga, but I have never seen them before. They were mostly found on the western shores of Kaliron.
现在我亲眼见到他们了.他们正在东边的海岸!看来只是一小队,大概是斥候,不过我们不欢迎他们,尤其是知道他们在西部干了什么后.干掉他们!告诉他们我们的态度!
I have seen them with my own eyes now. They have taken up residence along our shores here on the east! While it only seems to be a small group, probably scouts, they are not welcomed here. Not after what they have done in the west. Slay them all! Show them they are not welcome here!
我在整个卡利隆旅行研究动物和昆虫,我非常熟悉它们的生活习性.但是在数年前的战争后,看来一切都改变了.
I have studied all sorts of animals and insects, and have traveled all over Kaliron to do so. I am very familiar with all sorts of life and their behaviors. But everything I have known has seemed to change after the war several years ago.
那些蝎子不光长得更大,也更凶暴了.我从没见过这样的事情.也许你能帮我收集些它们的血液让我和之前的数据对比一下.3瓶足够了.
Not only have these scorpions grown in size to giant-like insects, they have also grown in their aggression. I have never seen such things before. You must collect samples of their blood for me so I can run tests and compare it to my old data. 3 vials should be enough.
我和我的姐姐一起试图找出荒地的野生动物发生了什么.对于生物学她比我知道的多得多,不过我还是能帮上忙的.
I am working with my sister trying to figure out some of the issues going on with the wildlife here in the Barrens. She knows so much more about biology than me, but I can still help her perform the mundane tasks.
我在研究狼的变化.它们变得大而且凶暴.请带给我3瓶狼血让我分析一下.
I am studying the changes in the coyotes. The have grown in size and become very aggressive. Bring me 3 vials of their blood so I can analyze it, please.
我受够这些人马了!它们除了骚扰我们什么都不干.
I have had it with these centaur! They have done nothing but hassle us. Our forces are spread thin enough as it is.
去扎哈拉荒地杀掉一些人马,我们要告诉它们我们可不害怕他们!
By venturing out into the Jahara Barrens and killing off some of them, we will show them that we are not afraid!
很高兴看到你这么快就到了.我没有时间很快告诉你发生了什么,但是我们真的很需要你的帮助.我们的商队带着瓦解之球前往了东方之路.他们打算用那个球破坏魔法障碍.
Glad you got here so quickly. I don't have time to bring you fully up to speed on what is going on here, but we need your assistance badly. We have sent out a caravan to the Eastern Road to the south east with a magical orb of dispelling. They were supposed to use the orb and try to break that magical barrier.
我们没有收到商队的任何回音.我们需要你前往东方之路搜寻商队... 或者找出发生了什么.如果商队被半人马袭击了,看看你能不能找到那个球,把它带去东方之路的魔法障碍.看看球是否有效是最首要的.
We have not heard back from the caravan or any of its members. We need you to travel down the path towards the Eastern Road and find that caravan... or find out what happened to it. If the caravan was destroyed by centaur, see if you can locate that orb and bring it to the barrier at Nebu. Knowing if the orb has any effect on the barrier is a top priority.
炼金术士不是总在制造药剂或者药膏的.很多时候你需要学习并从事科技工作.现在我在尝试找出野生生物变化的原因.
Being an Alchemist doesn't always mean creating potions and salves. Sometimes you do studies and scientific work. Right now I have been trying to figure out what caused the behavior pattern changes in the desert life here.
从两个绿洲各收集一份水样带给我.水是最可能的元凶.
Collect two water samples, one from each oasis and bring them back to me. It is quite possible that something in the water is corrupting the life here in the barrens.
半人马是有领导者的.它们自称为领主.我们需要干掉这些领主让它们陷入混乱.
The centaurs have a chain of command, believe it or not. They call themselves Lords. We need to eliminate these Lords and send their ranks into disarray.
首先,我们需要引出那些领主.找到它们的营地并屠杀半人马.这应该能引出那些领主.杀掉全部4个领主并向我汇报.
First, we need to draw out these Lords. Find their camps in the barrens and start killing all the centaur. This should draw out the Lords. Slay all four lords then return to me.
该死的半人马....
Damn centaur....
看!它们回来了!我们需要先解决这次入侵.武装起来!
Look! They are coming back! We will talk after this invasion. TO ARMS!
看!它们回来了!我们需要先解决这次入侵.武装起来.
Look! They are coming back! We will talk after this invasion. TO ARMS!
既然最有威胁的家伙已经被除掉了,我们可以试试看了.去沃姆森林里的悬崖寻找一处石头祭坛.在那里使用这根法杖.这会把雷诺兹召唤到那里让他调查祭坛.我们认为祭坛和豺狼人的进攻有关.
My colleague and I are discussing ideas and thoughts on why the gnolls suddenly became so aggressive. We have a few theories, but right now it is too dangerous for us to go out into the field and test these ideas.
因为需要派人调查,我现在腾不出人手.

他被黑寡妇咬了.他中毒很深,但是我们还有救他的机会...
This man has been bitten by the Black Widow. Her poison is quite deadly, but we can still save him...
如果你能拿到黑寡妇的毒囊,我就能制造出解毒剂救他.

当... 队伍... 进... 洞穴... 什么都... 巢穴... 可怕.... 蜘蛛....

再次向你问好.也许你现在不认识我.上次我们见面时我有具叫做黑格加特的躯体.我为早先的进攻道歉.我没法详细的解释,不过请远离祭坛的魔法.现在我正在墓地里尝试修复一些损害.
Hello again. You probably don't recgonize me in this form. The last time we meet I was possessing Haggart's body. My apologies for the aggression earlier. I can't explain in detail now, but the magic at that altar in the forest must be left alone. Currently I am trying to reverse some of the damage here at the graveyard.
我是守卫幽灵.我来到这里希望能纠正一些错误.我这么做已经有几个世纪了.因为我的力量被限制了,我似乎做不了什么.我一直在寻找能帮我的人.而你来了!
I an a protector spirit. I wander the land trying to help correct things that have gone wrong. I have done this for centuries. While my powers are limited, I can do small tasks that make a difference. I always seek aid of corporeal beings to help me complete these tasks. This is where you come in!
拿着这个分散之杖去被暗黑力量感染的坟墓. 这可以逼迫那些灵魂实体化.打败那些灵魂让他们安息.
Take this Wand of Dispersion and bring it to grave sites that are disrupted by dark energy. When you use the wand near one of these dark energy clusters it will force the spirit to enter our realm. Defeat the spirit to put it to rest.
灵魂们还没到这里,不过不远...最悲剧的就是它们曾经是我们的朋友们....
The spirits haven't come up this far in quite some time, but they are still out there... The worst part is these spirits used to be our friends and allies....
如果你能超度那些灵魂,它们就能安宁的离开了.对着阵亡的士兵用这根杖.从可怕的命运中拯救他们.
If you can release their spirits into the afterlife, they won't linger around and become angry and loathe the living. Take this wand and use it on any fallen soldier you find. Save them from this horrible fate.
欢迎来我们的城市,人类.感谢你破坏了沙尘暴.虽然那只是我们的麻烦之一.就像你的城市一样,我们也有一堆麻烦. 最首要的是从人马那里夺回圣石.

神庙现在有另一个问题,它被娜迦占据了.他们的黑暗魔法控制了神庙里的灵魂.我们需要清除神庙里的那加.你能帮我们么?
The defilement of our tomb is just another one of our problems, the Temple has also been taken over by Naga. Their dark magics have taken control of the spirits inside. We need to push through and remove the Naga presence from our sacred temple. Think you can help us out?

Insert this stone into the pillar to open the tomb.

唯一解救他灵魂的方法是摧毁他的物理形态. 打破中间大厅的符文.找到穆瓦奇并打败他.
The only way to free his spirit is to destroy the physical manifestation so the spirit can be released. Break the seals to the central chamber, find Muarki and destroy his physical presence.
萨满教的支持被刻在石板上保存在这个墓穴好多年.我们必须在这些石板被破坏前取回他们.
The shamanistic ways have been recorded on tablets over the years. The knowledge has been stored all throughout the tomb. With the presence here, we need to recover those tablets before they are destroyed.
找到8块石板并把他们取回来给我.
Search the tomb for the 8 tablets and return them safely to me.
火焰领主阿诺斯曾经是我们非常崇敬的人.但是现在...
This tomb has always been split into the warrior and mystical paths. But it was only recently the paths became corrupted and turned against us. We used to worship Avnos, pray to him before our battles, ask him to give us the strength to defeat our enemies... Much has changed now...
我们必须打败火焰领主阿诺斯.在他进攻我们之前.

冰霜领主卡诺斯曾经是我们非常崇敬的人.但是现在.
Our mystics used to commune with Karnos, look to him for wisdom and knowledge of the arcane arts... Now we live in fear of him and his twisted ways.

很高兴看到你朋友. 你已经看到我在东方之路入口设置的路障了吗?
Greetings, friend. You have come to seek my wisdom regarding the barrier around the Eastern Road, yes?
古代的精灵似乎出了什么问题. 野兽开始暴走, 并侵犯人类. 黑暗开始环绕着我们. 如果不能找到事情的原因, 我们将会一直沦陷下去. 去古代峡谷, 你会发现一只强大的半人马战争领主! 击败他, 解救我们的城市脱离他的魔爪.

使用幻象坩埚来显示雕像部件的位置，挖出它并释放雕像的灵魂，只有这样我们才能进入里面

"卷轴"
"Scroll"
你好, 我是引路人. 我来帮助你更好的熟悉游戏, 并给与你一些指导.
Welcome to TKoK! To get familiar with the game, it is recommended for new players to read these guidelines.
|cffFFC125[输入|r -ii |cffFFC125打开或关闭引路人]|r
|cffFFC125[You can enter |r -ii |cffFFC125to skip this guide permanently]|r
你的旁边是游戏指导员, 你可以查询游戏的一些基本情况. 当然, 我也会在之后的游戏中慢慢告诉你.
You are currently in the preparation area, next to the game instructor. You can check the basics by yourself of course, or I could tell you.
如果你对当前选择英雄不满意, 输入 -repick 来重新选择英雄. 虽然没有次数限制, 不过只可以在准备区这么做.
If you're not satisfied with your hero, you can use -repick to re-select another. There's no limit to the amount of repicks you can use, but you can't use it once you leave the preparation area.
如果你确认了你的英雄, 就离开准备区吧!
If you're sure of your choice, you can leave the preparation area!
恭喜你, 完成了走向卡利隆的第一步!
Congratulations on taking your first step in the Kingdom of Kaliron!
点击你的红十字, 然后在物品栏选择角色管理, 点击天赋树, 来学习你的第一个技能. 你也可以输入 -tt 来打开天赋树.
Open your hero's Actions menu (red cross) and then select the red cross again to open your Inventory and Talent tree to learn your first skill. You can also use the command -tt to open it quicker.
点击交谈, 用交谈点击头上有黄色问号的NPC, 可以选择接受任务.
Use the Talk command in your hero inventory to speak to NPCs. If you talk to an NPC with a yellow exclamation mark above their heads, you can accept their quest.
在卡利隆王国里, 只要1人接受任务, 就相当于全队接受了. 你可以在F9里查看接受的任务.
In TKoK, quest progress is shared. As long as at least one person accepts it, all players have that quest. You can press F9 to view quests.
第一个任务, 寻找村长. 村长就在村子的左上角. 顺便说一句, 这个村子叫塔尔卡门.
The first quest is to speak to the Village Elder on the top left corner of the starting village, which is called Tol'Calm.
靠近村长, 即可完成任务.
Once you move close to the Elder, the quest will autocomplete.
在卡利隆王国里, 完成的任务奖励不会直接发放, 而是需要自己领取.
In TKoK, quest rewards won't be claimed automatically but need to be received manually by the player.
每个人都可以领取任务奖励, 别人不会领走你的奖励.
All players, however, can receive the same quest rewards.
输入 z 可以清除屏幕上的消息.
Use -clear to clear messages on the screen.
输入 -di 显示前5次引路人对话.
Enter -di to show the last 5 guide dialogs.
输入 -ri 重置引路人对话.
Enter -ri to reset guide dialog.
奥术师是强大的输出职业. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00奥术飞弹|r.
Arcanist is a strong damage mage. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Arcanic Missile|r.
开荒阶段中战士以坦克为主. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00盾击.
Warrior is a strong tank. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Shield Slam.
塑能师的输出能力毋庸置疑. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00灼烧.
Pyromancer is a frail but poweful offensive caster. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Ignition.
野蛮人同时具备输出和辅助能力. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00重斩.
Barbarians can deal great damage while also boosting allies. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Cleave.
德鲁伊有着不俗的输出能力. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00月火术.
Druid is versatile and powerful, but requires finesse to use. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Moonfire.
牧师是最强大的治疗职业. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00闪光术.
Cleric is the strongest healer. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Flash of Light.
暗影剑士的输出能力一鸣惊人. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00黑暗凋零
Shadowblade is a niche utility hero with moderate damage output. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Dark Blast.
混沌骑士是压制型坦克职业. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00意念之刃.
Chaotic Knight is a supportive tank. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Mindblade.
圣骑士兼顾辅助和治疗. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00圣光术.
Paladin is able to both damage enemies and heal allies. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Mark of Sanctuary.
水占师的辅助能力更甚于输出. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00水弹.
Hydromancer possesses strong suppportive skills. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Water Bolt.
幻影行者是强力的刺杀输出职业. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00邪恶打击.
Phantom Stalker has the strongest single-target damage output. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Gash.
游侠具有大范围输出能力. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00爆裂箭.
Ranger deals good damage over long range. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Explosive Arrow.
游医是兼顾输出的治疗职业. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00温柔治愈.
Medicaster is a strong AoE healer. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Tender Cure.
毒灵师具备强大的持续伤害输出. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00剧毒钉刺.
Venomancer possesses strong sustained damage output. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Toxic Nail.
裂空武士同时具有物理和魔法输出. 推荐1级学习|cFFFFFF00遥光斩.
Chronowarper deals both physical and magical damage. The first recommended skill to learn is |cFFFFFF00Lithosensing Slash.
推荐奥术师3感知1体质.
The recommended Arcanist stat distribution is 3 Wisdom and 1 Constitution every level.
推荐战士全体质.
The recommended Warrior stat distribution is full Constitution every level.
推荐塑能师3感知1体质.
The recommended Pyromancer stat distribution is 3 Wisdom and 1 Constitution every level.
推荐野蛮人全强壮.
The recommended Barbarian stat distribution is 4 Strength every level.
推荐德鲁伊全感知.
The recommended Druid stat distribution is 3 Intelligence and 1 Constitution every level.
推荐牧师2感知2体质.
The recommended Cleric stat distribution is 2 Wisdom and 2 Constitution every level.
推荐暗影剑士3感知1体质.
The recommended Shadowblade stat distribution is 3 Dexterity and 1 Constitution every level.
推荐混沌骑士全体质.
The recommended Chaotic Knight stat distribution is full Constitution every level.
推荐圣骑士3感知1体质.
The recommended Paladin stat distribution is 3 Wisdom and 1 Constitution every level.
推荐水占师全感知.
The recommended Hydromancer stat distribution is 3 Wisdom and 1 Constitution every level.
推荐幻影行者3灵巧1体质.
The recommended Phantom Stalker stat distribution is 3 Dexterity and 1 Constitution every level.
推荐游侠全灵巧.
The recommended Ranger stat distribution is 3 Dexterity and 1 Constitution every level.
推荐游医2感知2精神.
The recommended Medicaster stat distribution is 2 Wisdom and 2 Spirit every level.
推荐毒灵师全感知.
The recommended Venomancer stat distribution is 3 Wisdom and 1 Constitution every level.
推荐裂空武士全强壮.
The recommended Chronowarper stat distribution is 2 Strength, 1 Wisdom and 1 Constitution every level.

推荐裂空武士2级学习|cFFFFFF00次元斩|r.
The recommended level 2 skill to learn for Chronowarper is |cFFFFFF00Dimensional Slash|r.
开荒阶段, 在提升重要属性的同时, 也建议加一些体质来弥补生命值不足.
While it is important to improve primary attributes, more Consitution is recommended if you find yourself dying too quickly.
在游戏后期, 你可以随意洗点, 来加最合理的属性点.
As you progress, you will be able to reset your stats and freely customize them according to your needs.
记住：属性点与装备配合才能发挥最大价值. 现在也许你不懂, 以后你会懂的~
Remember: You can change your equipment and stats together to try to achieve the best result.
完成任务后, 会触发接下来的剧情. 你可以接受新任务.
After the quest is completed, it will allow you to accept the next quest.
去找头上带有黄色问号的NPC交谈吧! 完成任务你将获得大量金钱和经验.
Go to the NPC with a yellow exclamation mark on their head! Completing the given quests will reward significant amounts of EXP and gold.
每级获得4属性点. 每2级获得1天赋点.
Each level, you gain 4 stat points and every 2 levels, you gain one talent point.
小镇的左边就是沃姆森林. 继续左走可以到达沃姆. 去之前不要忘记接受所有任务哦.
To the left of the starting town is Vormur Forest. Further left is the next town, Vormur. Before going, accept all the quests that you can!
点开动作菜单, 用互动里的互动(I)来点击大门, 即可打开大门.
Inside the Actions Menu, with the World Interactions command you are able to interact with the gate to open it.
在卡利隆王国中, 很多东西都可以互动. 这也是完成一些任务的关键!
In the Kingdom of Kaliron, many world objects can be interacted with this way. This is required for many quests!
你到了沃姆. 还记得传送门管理员的任务吗? 把你身上的卷轴交给这里的传送门管理员即可.
You are at Vormur. Remember the quest the Portal Master gave you? Here is where you will give the scroll to the Portal Master here.
你的游戏进度获得更新! 你可以使用传送门到塔尔卡门了. 输入-st来显示自己的游戏进度. 或者输入-sh对所有人显示.
Your game progress has been updated! You can now use the teleport between Tol'Calm and Vormur. You can enter -st to display your game progress, or -sh to display it to everyone.
游戏进度达到1, 你在下次读档后可以直接使用传送门到沃姆.
Game progress 1 corresponds to directly after unlocking the Vormur teleport gate.
保存游戏会保存你的游戏进度【二区自动保存】. 下次进入游戏后, 任务都会刷新. 不过你可以【跳过】并接受新的任务.
Saving your hero will also save your game progress. The next time you load, the quests will reset, but your available teleport gates will be remembered.
头上有白色问号的NPC可以交谈领取任务奖励. 每个人都要自己领取.
There is a white question mark over the head of any NPC with a quest reward. Every player should talk to the NPC to receive their reward.
你可以在动作菜单里查看有哪些任务你还没有领取奖励.
You can use the appropriate Actions Menu command to see which NPCs have available rewards.
任务奖励给了你很多金钱. 你可以考虑更新一下装备了. 在塔尔卡门商店购买装备.
Quest rewards give you significant amounts of gold and experience. Now that you have some gold, you can consider visiting the equipment shop at Tol'Calm if you haven't already.
你的钱也可以购买一些消耗品. 我强烈推荐你购买精神药剂, 可以在10分钟内不断恢复你的魔法值, 让你战斗更持久.
Gold can also be used to purchase consumables. It is recommended to purchase an Elixir of Spirit, as this will grant you mana regeneration to ensure you don't go out of mana too quickly.
注意: 不同的持续药剂不能叠加. 不要浪费钱.
You should note that Elixirs can't stack, nor can you have more than one active at any time.
卡利隆王国的第一个BOSS：育母蜘蛛就在塔尔卡门洞穴的最深处.
The first boss monster you'll encounter is in the deepest point of the Tol'Calm Caves: The Broodmother.
卡利隆王国的BOSS分为普通击杀和VX击杀. VX模式指的是完成某些条件来打倒BOSS. 具体细节可以在训练场NPC查看.
All bosses have optional objectives to complete during the boss fight. If completed, the boss drops more and better loot. This is called VX mode. You can view the conditions of VX modes for all bosses at the Training Grounds.
恭喜你击杀卡利隆的第一个BOSS! 不要忘记领取任务奖励.
Congratulations on defeating the first boss in your journey through Kaliron! Don't forget to take the quest reward and save your progress!
上面是统计数据. 你可以输入-ls来查看之前的统计数据.
Above is the statistics. You can enter -ls to view the last shown statistics.
卡利隆王国的BOSS只有在VX模式下才可以掉落史诗装备.
Only bosses killed in VX mode can drop Epic-quality or higher gear.
你可以使用传送卷轴来快速回城. 出门携带传送卷轴是个好习惯.
